      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Outlook</font></font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
outlook section contains a number of forward-looking statements, all of which
are based on current expectations.&#160;&#160;Actual results may differ
materially.&#160;&#160;Refer to the Safe Harbor Statement below as well as Risk
Factors and other <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">information
contained in our 2007 Annual Report on Form 10-K for information concerning the
key risks to achieving future performance goals.</font></font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
current business environment is characterized by significantly higher commodity
costs and increased competitive activity. For the full year 2008, we expect
increases in input costs versus 2007 of approximately $100 million, reducing
gross margin by 200 basis points. We will also incur higher costs for increased
investment in brand support and selling capabilities in the United States, while
we are taking steps to enhance product innovation across our portfolio. We will
also be continuing to invest in key international markets, particularly China
and India.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">To offset
higher input costs, we have increased the wholesale prices of our domestic
confectionery line and are implementing aggressive productivity and cost savings
initiatives in addition to those already underway as part of our global supply
chain transformation program. However, price increases and productivity
improvements will only partly offset input cost increases and expenses
associated with investment spending plans, resulting in lower EBIT and EPS,
excluding items affecting comparability.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We expect
consolidated net sales to grow 3% to 4% in 2008. We have introduced <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Hershey&#8217;s</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Bliss</font>&#8482; and Starbucks<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> branded
chocolates and will introduce <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Signatures</font> packaged candy
later this year to more fully participate in the rapidly growing premium and
trade-up segments of the chocolate category in the United States. For the
remainder of the Americas, we expect increases in net sales from our businesses
in Canada, Mexico, and Brazil, along with incremental sales from the Godrej
Hershey Ltd. acquisition.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For 2008,
we expect total pre-tax business realignment and impairment charges for our
global supply chain transformation program and restructuring our business in
Brazil to be in the range of $140 to $160 million. We expect costs of
approximately $85 million to be included in cost of sales, primarily for
accelerated depreciation, and approximately $20 million to be included in
selling, marketing and administrative expenses for start up costs and program
management. The remainder of these costs will be included in business
realignment and impairment charges. Total charges associated with our business
realignment initiatives in 2008 are expected to reduce earnings per
share-diluted by $0.37 to $0.42.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As a
result of higher input costs and increased investment in trade and consumer
promotional programs and advertising, along with investment in our international
businesses, we expect EBIT to decrease in 2008, excluding the impact of business
realignment and impairment charges. We expect EBIT margin to decline due to
investments in advertising, selling capabilities and building infrastructure for
our international businesses.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Business
realignment and impairment charges associated with our global supply chain
transformation program and the restructuring of our business in Brazil will
reduce net income and earnings per share in 2008. Excluding the impact of these
business realignment initiatives, net income is expected to decline reflecting
the increased investments in our businesses. As a result, earnings per
share-diluted excluding items affecting comparability is expected to be within
the $1.85 to $1.90 range for 2008.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A
reconciliation of GAAP and non-GAAP items to the Company&#8217;s earnings per
share-diluted outlook is as follows:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We are
subject to changing economic, competitive, regulatory and technological
conditions, risks and uncertainties because of the nature of our operations. In

3.&#160;&#160;Quantitative and Qualitative Disclosures About Market
Risk</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
potential net loss in fair value of foreign exchange forward contracts of ten
percent resulting from a hypothetical near-term adverse change in market rates
was $.2&#160;million as of March 30, 2008 and December&#160;31,
2007.&#160;&#160;The market risk resulting from a hypothetical adverse market
price movement of ten percent associated with the estimated average fair value
of net commodity positions increased from $31.7 million as of December 31, 2007,
to $38.5&#160;million as of March 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;Market risk represents
10% of the estimated average fair value of net commodity positions at four dates
prior to the end of each period.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
4.&#160;&#160;Controls and Procedures</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Disclosure
controls and procedures are controls and other procedures that are designed to
ensure that information required to be disclosed in our reports filed or
submitted under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (the "Exchange Act") is
recorded, processed, summarized and reported within the time periods specified
in the Securities and Exchange Commission's rules and
forms.&#160;&#160;Disclosure controls and procedures include, without
limitation, controls and procedures designed to ensure that information required
to be disclosed in our reports filed under the Exchange Act is accumulated and
communicated to management, including the Company's Chief Executive Officer and
Chief Financial Officer, as appropriate, to allow timely decisions regarding
required disclosure.</font></div>

controls and procedures are effective.&#160;&#160;There has been no change

    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">Exhibit 10.1<br></div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">FIRST
AMENDMENT TO</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">THE
HERSHEY COMPANY</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">EXECUTIVE
BENEFITS PROTECTION PLAN</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(GROUP
3A)</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Amended
and Restated as of October&#160;2, 2007)</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
The Hershey Company (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) currently maintains The Hershey Company
Executive Benefits Protection Plan (Group&#160;3A) (Amended and Restated as of
October&#160;2, 2007), (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;);</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
the Board of Directors of the Company (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) approved the amendment of
the Plan, effective February&#160;13, 2008, to reduce the severance benefits
payable under the Plan with respect to the qualifying termination of employment
after a change in control of the Company; and</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
this amendment shall supersede the provisions of the Plan to the extent those
provisions are inconsistent with the provisions of this amendment.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NOW,
THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED that, by virtue and in exercise of the power reserved
to the Board by Article&#160;7 of the Plan, the Plan is hereby amended,
effective February&#160;13, 2008, by amending Section 1.36, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Severance Period</font>, to
read as follows:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;1.36&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Severance Period</font>
means the period beginning on the Executive&#8217;s Date of Termination and continuing
for 24 months, or, if less, the number of months until the Executive would reach
his or her Mandatory Retirement Age, if applicable, but not less than 12
months.&#8221;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">IN
WITNESS WHEREOF, the Company has caused this amendment to be executed effective
as of February&#160;13, 2008.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="39%" style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 2px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="39%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">THE
      HERSHEY COMPANY</font></div>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">By:&#160;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline">&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">/s/
      Burton H.
      Snyder&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18.7pt"></font>Burton H. Snyder</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18.7pt"></font>Senior Vice
      President,</font></div>

<DESCRIPTION>AMENDED DIRECTORS COMPENSATION PLAN
<TEXT>
<html>
  <head>

<!-- Licensed to: THE HERSHEY COMPANY-->
<!-- Document Created using EDGARizer 4.0.5.0 -->

    <body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right">Exhibit
10.3</div>
    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br><br>&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">THE </font>HERSHEY <font style="DISPLAY: inline">COMPANY</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">DIRECTORS&#8217;
COMPENSATION PLAN</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="center">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Amended
and Restated as of February 13, 2008)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PURPOSE</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
purposes of the Directors' Compensation Plan (&#8220;Plan&#8221;) are to provide Directors
of <font style="DISPLAY: inline">The </font>Hershey <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company (&#8220;Company</font>&#8221;) with payment alternatives for
the retainer and fees payable for services as members of the Board of Directors
(&#8220;Board&#8221;) of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> or as a chair of
any committee thereof (together, &#8220;Director Fees&#8221;), to provide Directors the
opportunity to elect to receive all or a portion of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Directors Fees</font> in Deferred Stock Units (&#8220;DSUs&#8221;),
each representing an obligation of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> to issue one share of Common Stock of the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, $1.00 par value per share (&#8220;Common
Stock&#8221;), and to promote the identification of interests between such Directors
and the stockholders of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> by
paying a portion of each Director&#8217;s compensation in Restricted Stock Units
(&#8220;RSUs&#8221;), each RSU representing an obligation of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> to issue one share of Common
Stock.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 9pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ELIGIBILITY</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Any
Director of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> who is not an
employee of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> or any of its
subsidiaries shall be eligible to participate in the Plan.&#160;&#160;Except as
the context may otherwise require, references in this Plan to a &#8220;Director&#8221; shall
mean only those directors of the Company who are participants in the
Plan.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PAYMENT</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Director Fees.</font>&#160;A
Director shall be entitled to Director Fees, in such amounts as shall be
determined by the Board, for services on the Board and as a chair of any
committee of the Board.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Pursuant to
Section 4 hereof, a Director may elect to have payment of Directors Fees made
currently in cash and/or Common Stock or deferred for subsequent payment in cash
or Common Stock; provided that if paid currently, fees</font> payable for
services as a chair of any committee of the Board shall be payable only in
cash.&#160;&#160;Any shares of Common Stock payable under this Section 3(a)
shall be paid by the issuance to the Director of a number of shares of Common
Stock equal to the cash amount of the retainer so payable divided by the Fair
Market Value of one share of the Common Stock, as defined in Section 12
hereof.&#160;&#160;Any fractional share</font><br></div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-1-&#160;
</font></div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">of Common
Stock resulting from such payment shall be rounded to the nearest whole
share.&#160;&#160;The <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall issue
share certificates to the Director for the shares of Common Stock acquired or,
if requested in writing by the Director and permitted under such plan, the
shares acquired shall be added to the Director's account under the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>'s Automatic Dividend Reinvestment
Plan.&#160;&#160;As of the date on which the part or whole of the retainer is
payable in shares of Common Stock, the Director shall be a stockholder of the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> with respect to such
shares.&#160;&#160;Unless otherwise elected in Section 4, any remaining Director
Fees shall be payable in cash.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Restricted Stock
Units.</font>&#160;&#160;A Director shall also be entitled to receive RSUs, in
such amounts as shall be determined by the Board, for services on the
Board.&#160;&#160;Beginning <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">January</font>
1, 2008 and thereafter, unless otherwise directed by the Board, RSUs having a
value of $30,000 (or such other amount as the Board shall from time to time
determine) shall be awarded to each Director on the first day of January, April,
July<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">and</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
October</font>.&#160;&#160;The number of full and fractional RSUs so awarded
shall be determined by dividing $30,000 (or such <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">other</font> amount) by
the average of the per share closing price of the Common Stock on the New York
Stock Exchange as published in <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Wall Street Journal</font> (or such other reliable <font size="+0" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">publication</font>
</font>as the Board or its delegates may determine) for the last three trading
days of the month preceding the date of the award.&#160;&#160;Directors whose
membership on the Board commences after <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">January
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1,</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2008</font>
on a day which is not the first day of any January, April, July or October,
shall be awarded a pro rata number of RSUs with respect to the quarter during
which the Director joined the Board equal to the number of RSUs awarded to each
Director who was a member of the Board on the first day of the applicable
quarter, multiplied by a fraction, the numerator of which equals the number of
days remaining in the quarter after the first day on which such Director became
a member of the Board, and the denominator being the total number of days in the
quarter.&#160;&#160;A Restricted Stock Unit Account shall be established on the
books of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company</font>
in the name of each Director. During the period of the Director&#8217;s membership on
the Board, the Director&#8217;s Restricted Stock Unit Account shall be subject to
credits, adjustment and substitution to reflect any dividend or other
distribution on the outstanding Common Stock or any split or consolidation or
other change affecting the Common Stock. Any such credit, adjustment or
substitution shall be made in a manner similar to that set forth in Section 6(a)
and 6(b) with respect to Deferred Stock Compensation Accounts.&#160;&#160;RSUs
awarded prior to January 1, 2008 shall vest upon termination of the <font size="+0" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Director&#8217;s</font>
</font>membership on the Board by reason of retirement, death or disability, or
such other circumstances as the Board, in its sole discretion, shall at any time
determine (provided that a termination of a <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Director&#8217;s</font>
membership on the Board following a Change in Control (as defined in the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company</font>&#8217;s
Executive Benefits Protection Plan (Group 3A), the &#8220;EBPP&#8221;) shall be considered a
retirement for this purpose).&#160;&#160;RSUs not vested upon or within 120 days
following the Director&#8217;s termination of membership on the Board, as aforesaid,
shall be forfeited as of 11:59 p.m. (Eastern Time) on the 120th day following
such Director&#8217;s termination of membership on the Board, as
aforesaid.&#160;&#160;The balance of the Director&#8217;s Restricted Stock Unit
Account which becomes vested upon termination of the Director&#8217;s membership shall
be paid in a lump sum in accordance with Section 7.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">RSUs
awarded for periods after 2007 (together with credits, adjustments or
substitutions attributable thereto, &#8220;Post-2007 RSUs&#8221;) shall vest upon the first
anniversary of the day upon which such Post-2007 RSUs were awarded, or such
other date or dates as set forth by the Board at the time of the award;
provided, that the vesting of such Post-2007 RSUs shall be accelerated to the
date of termination of the Director&#8217;s membership on the Board by reason of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">retirement,
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">death or
disability, or for any reason following a Change
in</font></font></font></font></div>

    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font size="+0"><font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font size="+0" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font size="+0" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Control
</font>(</font>as defined in the Company&#8217;s Executive Benefits Protection Plan
(Group 3A), the &#8220;EBPP&#8221;), or such other circumstances as the Board, in its sole
discretion, shall at any time </font></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">determine.
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For
purposes of this Plan, termination of a director&#8217;s membership on the Board at
anytime following the director&#8217;s 60</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">th</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">birthday
shall be deemed a retirement.&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
portion of a </font></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Director&#8217;s
Restricted Stock Unit Account attributable to Post-2007 RSUs which becomes
vested in accordance with the </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">second
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">preceding
sentence shall, unless deferred by the Director into the Director&#8217;s Deferred
Stock Compensation Account pursuant to an election made under Section 4, be paid
in a lump sum in accordance with Section 7.</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font>If
payment hereunder would result in the issuance of a fractional share of Common
Stock, such fractional share shall not be issued and cash in lieu of such
fractional share shall be paid to the Director based upon the average of the per
share closing price of the Common Stock&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">on</font>
the New York Stock Exchange as published in <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Wall Street Journal</font> (or such other reliable publication as the Board or
its delegates may determine) for the three trading days immediately preceding
the date of payment.&#160;&#160;The <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company</font>
shall issue share certificates to the Director, or the Director&#8217;s designated
beneficiary, for the shares of Common Stock represented by the Director&#8217;s vested
RSUs, or if requested in writing by the Director and permitted under such plan,
the shares to be distributed shall be added to the Director&#8217;s account under the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company</font>&#8217;s
Automatic Dividend Reinvestment Plan. As of the date on which the Director is
entitled to receive payment of shares of Common Stock, a Director shall be a
stockholder of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company</font>
with respect to such shares.</font></font></font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ELECTIONS</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Director Fee Payment
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">and RSU
Payment</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Alternatives</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">.</font>&#160;&#160;A
Director may elect any one of the following alternatives with respect to payment
of Director Fees and with respect to payment of Post-2007 RSUs:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(1)&#160;&#160;
to receive currently full payment of Director Fees in cash and/or Common Stock,
as set forth in Section 3(a) above, on the date or dates on which the Director
Fees are payable;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(2)&#160;&#160;
to defer payment of all or a portion of the Director Fees for subsequent payment
in cash (a &#8220;Cash Deferral Election&#8221;);</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(3)&#160;&#160;
to defer payment of all or a portion of the Director Fees for subsequent
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">payment
in shares of Common Stock (a &#8220;Stock Deferral Election&#8221;); or</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 9pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(4)<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">to defer payment of all or a portion of the Post-2007
RSUs for subsequent payment in shares of Common Stock (also a
</font></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;Stock Deferral Election&#8221;); or</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 45pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;&#160;&#160; (5)&#160;&#160; </font>a combination
of (2), (3) and (4).&#160;&#160;</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Filing and Effectiveness of
Elections.</font>&#160;&#160;The election by a Director to receive payment of
Director Fees other than as set forth in Section 4(a)(1) on the date on which
the Director Fees<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">are otherwise payable, or to receive payment of shares
of Common Stock attributable to the vesting of Post-2007 RSUs other than on the
date which the shares</font> are otherwise payable is made by filing with the
Secretary of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> a Notice of
Election in the form prescribed by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> (an &#8220;Election&#8221;).&#160;&#160;In order to
be effective for any calendar year, an Election must be received by the
Secretary of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> on or before
December 31 of the preceding calendar year, except that if a Director files a
Notice of Election on or before 30 days subsequent to the Director's initial
election to the office of Director, the Election shall be effective on the date
of filing with respect to Director Fees <font style="DISPLAY: inline">and
Post-2007 RSUs</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>payable for any
portion of the calendar year which remains at the date of such
filing.&#160;&#160;An Election may not be modified or terminated after the
beginning of a calendar year for which it is effective.&#160;&#160;Unless
modified or terminated by filing a new Notice of Election on or before December
31 immediately preceding the calendar year for which such modification or
termination is effective, an Election shall be effective for and apply to
Director Fees payable for each subsequent calendar year.&#160;&#160;Director
Fees earned <font style="DISPLAY: inline">or Post-2007 RSUs which
vest</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>at any time for which an
Election is not effective shall be paid as set forth in Section 4(a)(1) on the
date when the Director Fees <font style="DISPLAY: inline">or Section 7 on the
date the shares attributable to such Post-2007 RSUs</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>are otherwise payable<font style="DISPLAY: inline">, as applicable</font>.&#160;&#160;Any Election shall
terminate on the date a Director ceases to be a member of the Board.
&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Cash Deferral
Elections.</font>&#160;&#160;Director Fees deferred pursuant to a Cash Deferral
Election shall be deferred and paid as provided in Sections 5 and
7.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Stock Deferral
Elections.</font>&#160;&#160;Director Fees<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">and Post-2007
RSUs</font> deferred pursuant to a Stock Deferral Election shall be deferred and
paid as provided in Sections 6 and 7.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">5</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">DEFERRED
CASH COMPENSATION ACCOUNT</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">General.</font>&#160;&#160;The
amount of any Director Fees deferred in accordance with a Cash Deferral Election
shall be credited on the date on which such Director Fees are otherwise payable
to a deferred cash compensation account maintained by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> in the name of the Director (a &#8220;Deferred
Cash Compensation Account&#8221;).&#160;&#160;A separate Deferred Cash </font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Compensation
Account shall be maintained for each calendar year for which a Director has
elected a different number of payment installments or as otherwise may be agreed
between the </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Director
and the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Adjustment for Earnings or
Losses.</font>&#160;&#160;The amount in the Director's Deferred Cash
Compensation Account shall be adjusted to reflect net earnings, gains or losses
in accordance with the provisions of <font style="DISPLAY: inline">The</font>
Hershey <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> Deferred Compensation Plan
relating to Investment Credits and Investment Options.&#160;&#160;The adjustment
for earnings, gains or losses shall be equal to the amount determined under (1)
below as follows:&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>

        </div>

    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="center">
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right">
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Deemed
Investment Options.</font>&#160;&#160;The total amount determined by multiplying
the rate earned (positive or negative) by each fund available (taking into
account earnings distributed and share appreciation (gains) or depreciation
(losses) on the value of shares of the fund) for the applicable period by the
portion of the balance in the Director's Deferred Cash Compensation Account as
of the end of each such period, respectively, which is deemed to be invested in
such fund pursuant to paragraph (2) below.&#160;&#160;Subject to elimination,
modification or addition by the Board, the funds available for the Director's
election of deemed investments pursuant to paragraph (2) below shall be <font style="DISPLAY: inline">one or more of</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>the funds available (excluding Common
Stock) under the Investment Options of <font style="DISPLAY: inline">The</font>
Hershey <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> Deferred Compensation
Plan</font><br>&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Deemed
Investment Elections.</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(A)&#160;&#160;The
Director shall designate, on a form prescribed by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, the percentage of the deferred Director
Fees that are to be deemed to be invested in the&#160; available funds under
paragraph (1) above.&#160;&#160;Said designation shall be effective on a date
specified <font style="DISPLAY: inline">therein</font> and remain in effect and
apply to all subsequent deferred Director Fees until changed as provided
below.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(B)&#160;&#160;A
Director may elect to change, on a calendar year basis (or on such other basis
as permitted from time to time by the Board), the deemed investment election
under paragraph (A) above with respect to future deferred Director Fees among
one or more of the options then available by written notice to the Secretary of
the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, on a form prescribed by the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> (or by voice or other form of
notice permitted by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>), at least
ten days before the first day of the calendar year for which the change is to be
effective, with such change to be effective for Director Fees credited to the
Deferred Cash Compensation Account on and after the effective date of the
change.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(C)&#160;&#160;
A Director may elect to reallocate the balance of his Deferred Cash Compensation
Account, subject to limitations imposed by the Board, on a calendar year
basis,&#160;&#160;among the deemed investment options then
available.&#160;&#160;A Director may make such an election by written notice to
the Secretary of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, on a form
prescribed by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> (or by voice or
other form of </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">notice
permitted by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>), at least ten
days before the first day of the calendar year for which the transfer election
is to be effective, with such </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">transfer
to be based on the value of the Deferred Cash Compensation Account on the last
day of the calendar year preceding the effective date of the transfer
election.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(D)&#160;&#160;The
election of deemed investments among the options provided above shall be the
sole responsibility of each Director.&#160;&#160;The <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> and Board members are not authorized to
make any recommendation to any Director with respect to such
election.&#160;&#160;Each Director assumes all risk connected with any
adjustment to the value of his Deferred Cash Compensation
Account.&#160;&#160;Neither the Board nor the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> in any way guarantees against loss or
depreciation.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-5-</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(E)&#160;
All payments from the Plan shall be made pro-rata from the portion of the
Director's Deferred Cash Compensation Account which is deemed to be invested in
such funds as may be available from time to time for deemed investment elections
under the Plan.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(F)&#160;
The <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall not be required or
obligated to invest any amounts in the funds provided as deemed investment
options, and such funds shall be used solely to measure investment
performance.&#160;&#160;Further, the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall not be precluded from providing for
its liabilities hereunder by investing in such funds or in any other investments
deemed to be appropriate by the Board.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Manner of
Payment.</font>&#160;&#160;The balance of a Director's Deferred Cash
Compensation Account will be paid to the Director or, in the event of the
Director's death, to the Director's designated beneficiary, in accordance with
the Cash Deferral Election.&#160;&#160;A Director may elect at the time of
filing the Notice of Election for a Cash Deferral Election to receive payment of
the Director Fees in annual installments rather than a lump sum, provided that
the payment period for installment payments shall not exceed fifteen years
following the Payment Commencement Date, as described in Section 7
hereof.&#160;&#160;The amount of any installment shall be determined by
multiplying (i) the balance in the Director's Deferred Cash Compensation Account
on the date of such installment by (ii) a fraction, the numerator of which is
one and the denominator of which is the number of remaining unpaid installments
(including the installment payment then being determined).&#160;&#160;The
balance of the Deferred Cash Compensation Account shall be appropriately reduced
on the date of payment to the Director or the Director's designated beneficiary
to reflect the installment payment made hereunder.&#160;&#160;Amounts held
pending distribution pursuant to this Section 5(c) shall continue to be credited
with the earnings, gains or losses as described in Section 5(b)
hereof.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 9pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">6</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">DEFERRED
STOCK COMPENSATION ACCOUNT</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">General.</font>&#160;&#160;The
amount of any Director Fees deferred in accordance with a Stock Deferral
Election shall be credited to a deferred stock compensation account maintained
by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> in the name of the Director
(a &#8220;Deferred Stock Compensation Account&#8221;).&#160;&#160;A separate Deferred Stock
Compensation Account shall be maintained for each calendar year for which a
Director has elected a different number of payment installments or as otherwise
determined by the Board.&#160;&#160;On each date on which Director Fees <font style="DISPLAY: inline">and/or Post-2007 RSUs become vested and</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>are otherwise payable and a Stock Deferral
Election <font style="DISPLAY: inline">applicable to such Directors Fees and/or
Post-2007 RSUs</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>is effective for
a Director, the Director's Deferred Stock Compensation Account for that calendar
year shall be credited with a number of full and fractional Deferred Stock Units
(&#8220;DSUs&#8221;) equal<font style="DISPLAY: inline">, in the case of Directors
Fees,</font> to the cash amount of the Director Fees payable divided by the Fair
Market Value of one share of the Common Stock, as defined in Section 12 hereof,
on the date on which such Director Fees are payable<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">and, in the
case of Post-2007 RSUs, to the number of Post-2007 RSUs which became vested and
were otherwise payable</font>.&#160;&#160;If a dividend or distribution is paid
on the Common Stock in cash or property other than Common </font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-6-</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Stock, on
the date of payment of the dividend or distribution to holders of the Common
Stock each Deferred Stock Compensation Account shall be credited with a number
of full and fractional DSUs equal to the number of full and fractional DSUs
credited to such Account on the date fixed for determining the stockholders
entitled to receive such dividend or distribution times the amount of the
dividend or distribution paid per share of Common Stock divided by the Fair
Market Value of one share of Common Stock, as defined in Section 12 hereof, on
the date on which the dividend or distribution is paid<font style="DISPLAY: inline">, it being intended that the number of full and
fractional DSUs credited as a result of the dividend or distribution shall be
equal to the number of full and fractional shares that would be issued if the
DSUs credited to the Account were actual shares participating in the Company&#8217;s
dividend reinvestment plan</font>.&#160;&#160;If the dividend or distribution is
paid in property, the amount of the dividend or distribution shall equal the
fair market value of the property on the date on which the dividend or
distribution is paid.&#160;&#160;The Deferred Stock Compensation Account of a
Director shall be charged on the date of distribution with any distribution of
shares of Common Stock made to the Director from such Account pursuant to
Section 6(c) hereof.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Adjustment and
Substitution.</font>&#160;&#160;The number of DSUs credited to each Deferred
Stock Compensation Account shall be proportionately adjusted to reflect any
dividend or other distribution on the outstanding Common Stock payable in shares
of Common Stock or any split or consolidation of the outstanding shares of
Common Stock.&#160;&#160;If the outstanding Common Stock shall, in whole or in
part, be changed into or exchangeable for a different class or classes of
securities of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> or securities of
another <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> or cash or property other
than Common Stock, whether through reorganization, reclassification,
recapitalization, merger, consolidation or otherwise, the Board shall adopt such
amendments to the Plan as it deems necessary to carry out the purposes of the
Plan, including the continuing deferral of any amount of any Deferred Stock
Compensation Account.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;(c)&#160;&#160;
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Manner of
Payment.</font>&#160;&#160;The balance of a Director's Deferred Stock
Compensation Account will be paid in shares of Common Stock to the Director or,
in the event of the Director's death, to the Director's designated beneficiary,
in accordance with the Stock Deferral Election.&#160;&#160;A Director may elect
at the time of filing of the Notice of Election for a Stock Deferral Election to
receive payment of the shares of Common Stock credited to the Director's
Deferred Stock Compensation Account in annual installments rather than a lump
sum, provided that the payment period for installment payments shall not exceed
fifteen years following the Payment Commencement Date as described in Section 7
hereof.&#160;&#160;The number of shares of Common Stock distributed in each
installment shall be determined by multiplying (i) the number of DSUs credited
to such Director&#8217;s Deferred Stock Compensation Account on the date of payment of
such installment, by (ii) a fraction, the numerator of which is one and the
denominator of which is the number of remaining unpaid installments (including
the installment payment then being determined) and by rounding such result down
to the nearest whole number of shares.&#160;&#160;The balance of the number of
DSUs credited to such Director&#8217;s Deferred Stock Compensation Account shall be
appropriately reduced in accordance with this Section 6(c) to reflect the
installment payments made hereunder.&#160;&#160;DSUs remaining in a Deferred
Stock Compensation Account pending distribution of shares of Common Stock
pursuant to this Section 6(c) shall continue to be credited with respect to
dividends or distributions paid on the Common Stock pursuant to Section 6(a)
hereof and shall be subject to adjustment pursuant to Section 6(b) </font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-7-</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">hereof.&#160;&#160;If
a lump sum payment or the final installment payment hereunder would result in
the issuance of a fractional share of Common Stock, such fractional share shall
not be issued and cash in lieu of such fractional share shall be paid to the
Director based on the Fair Market Value of a share of Common Stock, as defined
in Section 12 hereof, on the date immediately preceding the date of such
payment.&#160;&#160;The <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall issue
share certificates to the Director, or the Director's designated beneficiary,
for the shares of Common Stock distributed hereunder, or if requested in writing
by the Director and permitted under such plan, the shares to be distributed
shall be added to the Director's account under the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>'s Automatic Dividend Reinvestment
Plan.&#160;&#160;As of the date on which the Director is entitled to receive
payment of shares of Common Stock, a Director shall be a stockholder of the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> with respect to such
shares.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">7</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PAYMENT
COMMENCEMENT DATE</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Payment
of amounts in a Restricted Stock Unit Account (<font style="DISPLAY: inline">which is vested or first becomes vested upon termination
of the Director&#8217;s membership on the Board</font>), Deferred Cash Compensation
Account or a Deferred Stock Compensation Account shall commence on the first
business day next succeeding the 89<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font> day
following the day on which the Director ceases to be a member of the Board for
any reason, including death or disability.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Payment of shares of Common Stock attributable to
Post-2007 RSUs which become vested prior to the termination of the Director&#8217;s
membership on the Board and for which the Director has not made
an</font></font>&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">effective Stock Deferral Election shall be paid in a
lump sum on or before the 90</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline"> day following the day on which such amounts vest.
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">The</font> Governance<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">Committee</font> of the Board may provide for the
accelerated payment of Deferred Cash Compensation Accounts and Deferred Stock
Compensation Accounts in one lump sum in connection with a <font style="DISPLAY: inline">change in control event within the meaning of the
regulations promulgated under Code Section 409A,</font> notwithstanding any
other payment options previously selected by a Director under his or her Cash
Deferral Elections and Stock Deferral Elections.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">8</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">BENEFICIARY
DESIGNATION</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A
Director may designate, in the Beneficiary Designation form prescribed by the
<font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, any person to whom payments of
cash or shares of Common Stock are to be made if the Director dies before
receiving payment of all amounts due hereunder.&#160;&#160;A beneficiary
designation will be effective only after the signed beneficiary designation form
is filed with the Secretary of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>
while the Director is alive and will cancel all beneficiary designations signed
and filed earlier.&#160;&#160;If the Director fails to designate a beneficiary,
or if all designated beneficiaries of the Director die before the Director or
before complete payment of all amounts due hereunder, any remaining unpaid
amounts shall be paid in one lump sum to the estate of the last to die of the
Director or the Director's designated beneficiaries, if any.</font></div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
