    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">9</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NON-ALIENABILITY
OF BENEFITS</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Neither
the Director nor any beneficiary designated by the Director shall have the right
to, directly or indirectly, alienate, assign, transfer, pledge, anticipate or
encumber (except by reason of death) any amount that is or may be payable
hereunder, nor shall any such amount be subject to anticipation, alienation,
sale, transfer, assignment, pledge, encumbrance, attachment, or garnishment by
creditors of the Director or the Director's designated beneficiary or to the
debts, contracts, liabilities, engagements, or torts of any Director or
designated beneficiary, or transfer by operation of law in the event of
bankruptcy or insolvency of the Director or any beneficiary, or any legal
process.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">10</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NATURE OF
ACCOUNTS</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Any
Restricted Stock Unit Account, Deferred Cash Compensation Account or Deferred
Stock Compensation Account shall be established and maintained only on the books
and records of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, and no assets
or funds of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> or the Plan or
shares of Common Stock of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall
be removed from the claims of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>'s
general or judgment </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">creditors
or otherwise made available until such amounts are actually payable to Directors
or their designated beneficiaries as provided herein.&#160;&#160;The Plan
constitutes a mere promise by the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>
to make payments in the future.&#160;&#160;The Directors and their designated
beneficiaries shall have the status of, and their rights to receive a payment of
cash or shares of Common Stock under the Plan shall be no greater than the
rights of, general unsecured creditors of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>.&#160;&#160;No person shall be entitled
to any voting rights with respect to shares credited to any RSU or Deferred
Stock Compensation Account which is not yet payable to a Director or the
Director's designated beneficiary.&#160;&#160;The <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> shall not be obligated under any
circumstance to fund its financial obligations under the Plan, and the Plan is
intended to constitute an unfunded plan for tax purposes.&#160;&#160;However,
the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> may, in its discretion, set
aside funds in a trust or other vehicle, subject to the claims of its creditors,
in order to assist it in meeting its obligations under the Plan, if such
arrangement will not cause the Plan to be considered a funded deferred
compensation plan under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as
amended.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">11</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADMINISTRATION
OF PLAN; HARDSHIP WITHDRAWAL</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Full
power and authority to construe, interpret, and administer the Plan shall be
vested in the Board.&#160;&#160;Decisions of the Board shall be final,
conclusive, and binding upon all parties.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the terms
of a Cash Deferral Election or a Stock Deferral Election made by a Director
hereunder, the Board may, in its sole discretion, permit the withdrawal of
amounts credited to a Deferred Cash Compensation Account or shares credited to a
Deferred Stock</font></div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">-9-</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Compensation
Account with respect to Director Fees previously payable, or permit the early
vesting and payment of RSUs previously awarded, upon the request of a Director
or the Director's representative, or following the death of a Director upon the
request of a Director's beneficiary or such beneficiary's representative, if the
Board determines that the Director or the Director's beneficiary, as the case
may be, is confronted with an unforeseeable emergency.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline">An</font> unforeseeable emergency is <font style="DISPLAY: inline">a</font> severe financial hardship to the Director <font style="DISPLAY: inline">resulting from illness or accident of the Director, the
Director&#8217;s spouse, beneficiary or dependent, loss of the Director&#8217;s property due
to casualty or similar extraordinary and unforeseeable circumstances beyond the
Director&#8217;s control, which hardship cannot be relieved through insurance,
cessation of deferrals under the Plan or liquidation of assets that would not
cause a severe financial hardship</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">.&#160;&#160;Cash needs arising from foreseeable events,
such as the purchase or building of a house or education expenses, will not be
considered to be the </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">result of an
unforeseeable financial emergency.</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>The Director or the Director's beneficiary
shall provide to the Board such evidence as the Board, in its discretion, may
require to demonstrate that such emergency exists and financial hardship would
occur if the withdrawal were not permitted.&#160;&#160;The withdrawal shall be
limited to the amount or to the number of shares, as the case may be, necessary
to meet the emergency.&#160;&#160;Payment shall be made as soon as practicable
after the Board approves the payment and determines the amount of the payment or
number of shares which shall be withdrawn.&#160;&#160;In the case of a hardship
withdrawal from the Deferred Cash Compensation Account or Deferred Stock
Compensation Account, payment shall be made in a </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">single
lump sum from the portion of the Deferred Cash Compensation Account or Deferred
Stock Compensation Account, as applicable, with the largest number and in
reverse order of installment payments, in each case in accordance with Section
5(b)(2)(E) if the distribution is from the Deferred Cash Compensation
Account.&#160;&#160;No Director shall participate in any decision of the Board
regarding such Director's request for a withdrawal under this Section
11.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">12</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">FAIR
MARKET VALUE</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Fair
Market Value of the Common Stock (&#8220;Fair Market Value&#8221;) <font style="DISPLAY: inline">on a single date shall be the closing price on the
applicable date (or if not a trading date, the next preceding trading date), and
Fair Market Value, where the determination is made over a period of more than
one day, </font>shall be the average of the closing price for all trading dates
for the applicable period covered by a payment.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline">For purposes of Section 3(a) and 6(a) hereof, the</font>
applicable period for a quarterly <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Directors
Fees</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>payment or credit shall be
the three calendar months immediately preceding the calendar month during which
the day on which the payment or credit is being made<font style="DISPLAY: inline">, and the</font> applicable period for a<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">Directors
Fees</font> payment relating to a period other than a quarter shall be
determined under similar principles.&#160;&#160;The closing price of the Common
Stock <font style="DISPLAY: inline">for a single date or</font> for each day
within the applicable period shall be as quoted in <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The Wall Street Journal</font> (or in
such other reliable publication as the Board or its delegate, in its discretion,
may determine to rely upon).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br></div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">SECURITIES
LAWS; ISSUANCE OF <font style="DISPLAY: inline">SHARES; NONCERTIFICATED</font>
SHARES</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
obligation of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> to issue or
credit shares of Common Stock under the Plan shall be subject to (i) the
effectiveness of a registration statement under the Securities Act of 1933, as
amended, with respect to such shares, if deemed necessary or appropriate by
counsel for the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>, (ii) the condition
that the shares shall have been listed (or authorized for listing upon official
notice of issuance) upon each stock exchange, if any, on which the Common Stock
shares may then be listed and (iii) all other applicable laws, regulations,
rules and orders which may then be in effect.&#160;&#160;If, on the date on
which any shares of Common Stock would be issued sufficient shares of Common
Stock are not available under the Plan or the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">Company</font> is not obligated to issue shares pursuant
to this Section 13, then no shares of Common Stock shall be issued but rather,
in the case of Common Stock to be issued currently, cash shall be paid in
payment of the Director Fees payable.&#160;&#160;The Board shall adopt
appropriate rules and regulations to carry out the intent of the immediately
preceding sentence if the need for such rules and regulations
arises.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline">To the extent the Plan provides
for issuance of share certificates to reflect the transfer of shares of Common
Stock, the transfer of such shares may be effected on a noncertificated or &#8220;book
</font></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">entry&#8221; basis.</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">14</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">GOVERNING
LAW</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
provisions of this Plan shall be interpreted and construed in accordance with
the laws of the State of Delaware.&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">15</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">EFFECTIVE
DATE; AMENDMENT AND TERMINATION</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Plan
was adopted by the Board on December 4, 1996, and became effective as of January
1, 1997.&#160;&#160;The Plan was <font style="DISPLAY: inline">previously</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>amended and restated effective October 2,
2001, <font style="DISPLAY: inline">December 3, </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">2002</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">, June 14,
2007, November 11, 2007 and December 4, 2007.</font>&#160;&#160;The Plan, as
amended and restated herein, shall be effective as of February 13,
2008.&#160;&#160;The Board may amend or terminate the Plan at any time, provided
that no such amendment or termination shall adversely affect rights with respect
to amounts or shares then credited to any Deferred Cash Compensation Account or
Deferred Stock Compensation Account.</font></div>

of 300,000 (reflecting prior stock splits and stock dividends and as shall be
adjusted and subject to adjustment to reflect future stock splits and stock

hereunder.&#160;&#160;Effective as of April 17, 2007, the crediting of RSUs and
the ability to make elections to receive Directors Fees in shares of Common
Stock or to defer payment of Directors Fees </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">and Post-2007 RSUs </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">and have such fees </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">and/or RSUs </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline">credited as DSUs shall constitute a non-employee
directors award under The Hershey Company Equity and Incentive Compensation Plan
(the &#8220;EICP&#8221;).&#160;&#160;This Plan and the related Notice of Election and other
documents contemplated hereunder shall constitute the award agreement for
purposes of the EICP and shares of Common Stock issued with respect to such
RSUs, Directors Fees or DSUs shall be deemed issued from the shares authorized
for issuance under the EICP.</font></font></div>

EXECUTIVE CONFIDENTIALITY AND RESTRICTIVE COVENANT AGREEMENT (the &#8220;Agreement&#8221;)
is entered into as of February 13, 2008 (the &#8220;Effective Date&#8221;), between The
Hershey Company, a Delaware corporation together with its subsidiaries and
affiliates and its and their respective successors and assigns (&#8220;Employer&#8221;), and
___________________ (&#8220;Executive&#8221;).</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
Executive currently serves, or is being hired or promoted to serve, in an
E-grade level position with Employer.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
Employer possesses certain valuable confidential, proprietary and/or trade
secret information (collectively, &#8220;Confidential Information,&#8221; as further defined
below) that gives Employer a competitive advantage.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
Employer has developed and maintained, at substantial expense and over a
considerable period of time, relationships with customers, suppliers, agents,
licensees, licensors and others that likewise give Employer a competitive
advantage (&#8220;Business Relationships&#8221;).</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
as a result of Executive&#8217;s past, future, and/or continued employment in an
E-grade level position with Employer, Executive has been and/or will continue to
be given access to, and will assist in, the development and maintenance of
Employer&#8217;s Confidential Information and Business Relationships, and it is the
parties&#8217; intent to continue to safeguard such Confidential Information and
Business Relationships both during and after the term of Executive&#8217;s employment
with Employer.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
Employer&#8217;s reputation and present and future competitive position are dependent
upon Employer&#8217;s ability to protect its interests in such Confidential
Information and Business Relationships.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NOW,
THEREFORE, in consideration of (i) Employer employing Executive in an E-grade
level position with Employer, (ii) Employer providing and continuing to provide
Executive access to such Confidential Information and Business Relationships,
(iii) Employer providing and continuing to provide Executive access to
specialized training, (iv) Employer making an award of performance stock units
(&#8220;PSUs&#8221;) to Executive under the 2008-2009 PSU cycle (the &#8220;2008-2009 PSU award&#8221;),
(v) Employer permitting Executive to participate in and defer the 2008-2009 PSU
award into the Deferred Compensation Plan of Employer, and/or (vi) for other
good and valuable consideration, the sufficiency and receipt of which are hereby
acknowledged, Employer and Executive agree as follows:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Non-Disclosure of
Confidential Information</font>.&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges that due to
the nature of his/her employment and the position of trust that he/she holds or
will hold with Employer, he/she will have special access to, learn, be provided
with, and in some cases will prepare and create for Employer, trade secrets and
other confidential and proprietary information relating to Employer&#8217;s business,
including, but not limited to,</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div><br>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>

        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"></font>&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">information
about Employer&#8217;s manufacturing processes; manuals, recipes and ingredient
percentages; engineering drawings; product and process research and development;
new product information; cost information; supplier data; strategic business
information; information related to Employer&#8217;s legal strategies or legal advice
rendered to Employer; marketing, financial and business development information,
plans, forecasts, reports and budgets; customer information; new product
strategies, plans and project activities; and acquisition and divestiture
strategies, plans and project activities (collectively, &#8220;Confidential
Information&#8221;).&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges and agrees that Confidential
Information, whether or not in written form, is the exclusive property of
Employer, that it has been and will continue to be of critical importance to the
business of Employer, and that the disclosure of it to, or use of it by,
competitors and others will cause Employer substantial and irreparable
harm.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, Executive will not, either during his/her
employment or at any time after the termination (whether voluntary or
involuntary, and regardless of reason) of such employment with Employer, use, or
disclose any Confidential Information relating to the business of Employer which
is not generally available to the public.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the
foregoing provisions of this Paragraph 1, Executive may disclose or use any such
information (i)&#160;when such disclosure or use may be required or appropriate
in the good faith judgment of Executive in the course of his/her employment with
Employer, (ii)&#160;when required by a court of law, by any governmental agency
having supervisory authority over Executive or the business of Employer, or by
any administrative or legislative body (including a committee thereof) with
apparent jurisdiction, or (iii)&#160;with the prior written consent of
Employer&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;) or Board of Directors (&#8220;Board&#8221;)
(provided that, if Executive is CEO, such consent must be by the
Board).&#160;&#160;Executive understands and agrees that his/her obligations
under this Agreement shall be in addition to, rather than in lieu of, any
obligations Executive may have under any applicable statute or at common
law.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Non-Competition</font>.&#160;&#160;Executive
acknowledges that Employer is engaged in the business of developing, producing,
marketing, selling and distributing confectionery, snack, better-for-you and
balanced nutrition products and chocolate-related grocery products (&#8220;Employer&#8217;s
Business&#8221;).&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges that due to the nature of his/her
employment with Employer, he/she has and will have special access to, contact
with, and Confidential Information about, Employer&#8217;s Business and Business
Relationships.&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges that Employer has incurred
considerable expense and invested considerable time and resources in developing
its Business Relationships, and that those Business Relationships are critical
to the success of Employer&#8217;s business.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, both (i) during
the term of his/her employment with Employer, and (ii) for a period of twelve
(12) months following the termination of his/her employment (whether voluntary
or involuntary, and regardless of reason), Executive, except in the performance
of his/her duties to Employer, shall not, in any geographic area where Employer
conducts business, without the prior written consent of Employer&#8217;s CEO or Board
(provided that, if Executive is CEO, such consent must be by the Board),
directly or indirectly serve or act as an officer, director, employee,
consultant, advisor, independent contractor, agent or representative for the
domestic or worldwide confectionery, snack, better-for-you, balanced nutrition,
or chocolate-related grocery businesses of any person or entity that is in
competition with any of the aspects of Employer&#8217;s Business. For purposes of
clarification, Executive will not be deemed to be involved in a business in
competition</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div><br>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>

          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2&#160;
</font></div>

            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">

</font></div>

      </div><br>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">with
Employer&#8217;s Business, and accordingly this paragraph 2 will not be violated, by
the Executive (A) providing services to a subsidiary, division or unit of an
entity (a &#8220;parent company&#8221;) that engages, directly or indirectly, in any
competitive business described above, so long as Executive and the subsidiary,
division or unit to which he/she is providing services do not engage in any such
competitive business, or (B) serving at the corporate level of a parent company
that engages, directly or indirectly, in any competitive business described
above, so long as the gross revenues from such competitive businesses
constituted less than 10% of consolidated annual gross revenues for the parent
company&#8217;s most recently completed fiscal year.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Non-Solicitation;
Non-Disparagement</font>.&#160;&#160;Both (i) during the term of his/her
employment by Employer, and (ii) for a period of 12 months following the
termination of his/her employment (whether voluntary or involuntary, and
regardless of reason), Executive, except in the performance of his/her duties to
Employer, shall not directly or indirectly (including as an officer, director,
employee, consultant, advisor, agent or representative), for himself/herself or
on behalf of any other person or entity:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">knowingly
recruit or solicit, or participate in recruiting or soliciting, any of
Employer&#8217;s employees, or communicate, except in the case of a reference
described in the last sentence of this paragraph, to any other person or entity
about the nature, quality or quantity of work, or any special knowledge or
personal characteristics, of any person employed by Employer.&#160;&#160;If
Executive should wish to discuss possible employment with any then-current
employee of Employer during the period set forth above, Executive may request
written permission to do so from the most senior human resources officer of
Employer who may, in his/her discretion, grant a written exception to the no
solicitation covenant set forth immediately above; provided, however, Executive
shall not discuss any such employment possibility with any such employee prior
to such permission.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the provisions of
this paragraph shall not be violated by (i) general advertising or solicitation
not specifically targeted at employees of Employer, (ii) Executive serving as a
reference, upon request, for any employee of Employer, or (iii) actions taken by
any person or entity with which Executive is associated if Executive is not
personally involved in any manner in the matter and has not identified such
employee for recruiting or solicitation; or</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
(b)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">make any
public statements that disparage Employer, its&#160;&#160;employees, officers,
directors, products or services, provided that,&#160;&#160;notwithstanding the
foregoing, truthful statements made in the course of sworn testimony in
administrative, judicial or arbitral proceedings (including, without limitation,
depositions in connection with such proceedings), normal competitive-type
statements, and statements made in the good faith performance of the Executive&#8217;s
duties to Employer shall not be subject to this clause.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
4.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Violation of Paragraphs 1, 2
or 3</font>.&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges Employer&#8217;s valid and protectable
interest in aligning the long-term interests of valued employees with those of
Employer by providing Executive an ownership interest in the Employer through
the 2008-2009 PSU award and otherwise, and likewise acknowledges Employer&#8217;s
valid and protectable interest in preventing former employees whose interests
become adverse</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div><br>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
        </div>

          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3&#160;
</font></div>

</font></div>
        </div>
      </div><br>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">to the
Employer from maintaining an ownership or other interest in the
Employer.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, Executive agrees that if he/she violates any
of paragraphs 1, 2 or 3 above (the date on which any such violation occurs is
the &#8220;Date of Breach&#8221;), Employer may, in its sole discretion, in addition to any
other remedies available to it at law or in equity:&#160;&#160;(a) cancel any
unvested portion of the 2008-2009 PSU award; (b) require Executive to pay
Employer the full value of any portion of the 2008-2009 PSU award that vested
within the twelve (12) months immediately preceding the Date of Breach; and/or
(c) require Executive to pay Employer the value of all gains on any portion of
the 2008-2009 PSU award that were realized within the twelve (12) month period
immediately preceding the Date of Breach.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
5.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Entire
Agreement</font>.&#160;&#160;Executive acknowledges and agrees that (a) this
Agreement includes the entire agreement and understanding between the parties
with respect to the subject matter hereof, and may be amended, modified or
changed only by a written instrument executed by Executive and Employer, and (b)
violation of paragraphs 1, 2 or 3 hereof may cause Executive to lose the right
to receive, or may obligate Executive to repay to Employer, amounts awarded or
accrued under various plans and programs of Employer as described in paragraph 4
and that, to the extent any effect of this Agreement upon such amounts may be
inconsistent with the terms and conditions of such plans or programs as in
effect on the date hereof, this Agreement shall constitute an amendment of such
terms and conditions and Executive&#8217;s consent thereto.&#160;&#160;No provision of
this Agreement may be waived except by a writing executed and delivered by the
party sought to be charged.&#160;&#160;Any such written waiver will be effective
only with respect to the event or circumstance described therein and not with
respect to any other event or circumstance, unless such waiver expressly
provides to the contrary.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the foregoing, this
Agreement shall not supersede the provisions of Section 3 of the Long-Term
Incentive Program Participation Agreement to which Executive may be a party
insofar as the terms thereof apply to awards and amounts other than the
2008-2009 PSUs.</font></div>

      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">6.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Miscellaneous</font>.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 81pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This

principles&#160;of&#160;&#160;conflict of laws.</font></div>

</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All
notices and other communications hereunder shall be in writing; shall be
